言之不可复者,yan'zhi'bu'ke'fu'zhe
燕之水萃下而弱,yan'zhi'shui'cui'xia'er'ruo
言至虚也,yan'zhi'xu'ye
言至也,yan'zhi'ye
言智者试之以官,yan'zhi'zhe'shi'zhi'yi'guan
言终,yan'zhong
言重本,yan'zhong'ben
言中正以蓄慎也,yan'zhong'zheng'yi'xu'shen'ye
严诛无赦,yan'zhu'wu'she
晏子识不仕与耕者之有善者,yan'zi'shi'bu'shi'yu'geng'zhe'zhi'you'shan'zhe
养二孤者二子无征,yang'er'gu'zhe'er'zi'wu'zheng

养老弱而勿通,yang'lao'ruo'er'wu'tong
阳气毕上,yang'qi'bi'shang

养人如养六畜,yang'ren'ru'yang'liu'chu

养桑麻,yang'sang'ma

阳为德,yang'wei'de

养之以德,yang'zhi'yi'de

养之以义,yang'zhi'yi'yi
